Harvard University's Tercentenary Celebration Bestows Honorary Degrees on Sixty-Six Individuals

Cambridge, Massachusetts, USA - Harvard University, the oldest and most renowned university in North America, held its tercentenary celebration ceremony the other day, which concluded today. At the end, President Roosevelt attended and delivered a speech in three capacities. Roosevelt was originally a graduate of Harvard University, served as the chairman of the Harvard University Tercentenary Celebration Committee, and is also the current President of the United States. In his speech, President Roosevelt stated, "In these times of turmoil and uncertainty, so-called 'freedom of thought' has been banished from most countries and has no place to stand. Only Harvard University and our United States can hold the torch of truth and never extinguish it. In short, truth is the greatest thing in the world, and only truth will ultimately prevail. I do not want you to merely view tolerance and peace as neutral and impartial virtues but rather as active and positive principles, so that it may be." This time, Harvard University, in celebration of its three-hundredth anniversary, has conferred honorary doctoral degrees on many of the world's most famous scholars, including those of England, Scotland, France, Italy, Switzerland, Japan, Argentina, Norway, Germany, and the Soviet Union. Also among them are nine world-renowned scholars from various countries who have won the Nobel Prize. Furthermore, before President Roosevelt visited the school today to deliver a speech, twenty-four Harvard University graduates presented a petition to the President requesting that he re-examine the Lowell Committee's report on the Sacco and Vanzetti case. Sacco and Vanzetti were both Italian-Americans who, due to their usual belief in anarchism, were resented by the authorities. Later, they were implicated in a terrorist act and imprisoned. The court sentenced them to death. At the time, American liberals repeatedly sought a retrial due to insufficient evidence. After several years, the original verdict was upheld. In August 1927, the death sentence was carried out. When the two convicts were not yet executed, the Americans organized a committee, chaired by Harvard University President Lowell. The committee's final report did not allow intervention to prevent the execution of the death sentence. Sacco and Vanzetti could not escape death. This is an old case from several years ago. (Havas dispatch, 18th)

Cambridge, Massachusetts, USA - After President Roosevelt visited Harvard University to deliver a speech during its tercentenary celebration, he returned to Washington immediately due to his wife's illness. Harvard University today presented honorary degrees to sixty-six world-renowned scientists and scholars, including fourteen from the United States, twelve from the UK, ten from Germany, six from France, five from Switzerland, three from Italy, two each from Japan, Denmark , Scotland and Swedan, and one each from the Netherlands, Argentina, Norway, Canada, Austria, Czechia, Australia and China. Among them are twelve Nobel Prize winners. (National News Agency dispatch, 18th)

Japan's Kanmon Strait Undersea Tunnel Construction Begins: Linking the Japanese Mainland with the Kyushu Railway

Moji - The groundbreaking ceremony for the Kanmon Strait Tunnel, which will connect the Japanese mainland with the Kyushu Railway, was held at Komorie-machi, Moji City, at 10:00 AM on the 19th. Deputy Railway Minister Tago, Parliamentary Councillor Hatayama, the governors of both Yamaguchi and Totsuka prefectures, the director of the Kitakyushu Improvement Office Nagamiya, and other related personnel, as well as over 300 dignitaries, attended and participated in the solemn ceremony. The ceremonial first dig was performed by the construction commander, Director Nagamiya, and the world-renowned and difficult project to tunnel under the strait was officially launched. The construction of the Kanmon Strait Tunnel, which is attracting attention from the world's academic community and is anticipated by the entire nation, has begun with excavation and tunneling from the Komorie side of Moji. (Domei News Agency dispatch, 19th)

European Troubles Multiply; League of Nations Seeks Respite; Proposal to Postpone Discussion of Covenant Amendment; Abyssinia to Be Denied Attendance

(Geneva) Amidst the repeated occurrence of the Danzig diplomatic turmoil and the escalation of the Spanish Civil War, the League of Nations Administrative Council held its 93rd session today to discuss the issue of maintaining world peace. However, it is unlikely to make any resolutions regarding Italy's annexation of Abyssinia and Germany's reoccupation of the Rhineland. It is generally believed that the Council intends to gain a respite at this session, hoping to gradually recover after the League of Nations' failure to resolve European issues. No Italian representatives attended today's meeting. However, after the General Assembly rejects the attendance of Abyssinian representatives next Monday, the Italian chief representative, Sir Aloisi, will lead his country's delegation to attend. He believes that the discussion of League of Nations reform will inevitably be postponed. (National Telegram, 18th)

(Geneva) The 93rd session of the League of Nations Administrative Council opened tonight, chaired by Chilean representative Mr. Figuna. The meeting was of a closed nature and began with the determination of the agenda. Based on the requests of the Iranian and Iraqi governments, it was decided not to include the border dispute between the two countries on the agenda. It was also decided to submit the document from the governments of 18 nations regarding the principles of implementing the League of Nations Covenant to the General Assembly. League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol delivered a statement describing his recent visit to Italy and reported to the Administrative Council on his meetings with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and Foreign Minister Ciano in Rome. It is said that Mussolini proposed conditions that Italy would only participate in this General Assembly if no Abyssinian representatives were present. He also stated that he had informed Mussolini that this issue must be decided by the General Assembly's Credentials Committee. It is rumored that the committee will point out that the Abyssinian government has largely failed to fulfill the conditions stipulated in the League of Nations Covenant. It is expected that a majority of countries in the General Assembly will approve this recommendation, allowing Italy to return to the League of Nations. Spanish representative de los Caballero, who currently serves as Foreign Minister in the Cabellero cabinet, lodged a serious protest today with French Foreign Minister Delbos regarding Portugal's continued violation of neutrality obligations in the Spanish Civil War. Mr. Delbos also acknowledged the inappropriateness and intolerability of Portugal's attitude. (Reuters Telegram, 18th)

Then, it will temporarily adjourn and reconvene after the opening of the League of Nations General Assembly next Monday. When the League of Nations General Assembly convenes next Monday, it will appoint special members to review the credentials of the representatives of various countries. French Premier Invites British Foreign Secretary to Meet; Discussion of Five-Power Conference Issues

(London) According to official sources, British Foreign Secretary Eden, at the suggestion of French Premier Léon Blum, will pass through Paris when traveling to Geneva to attend the League of Nations General Assembly, to hold talks with key figures in the French government. The purpose of the talks is regarding preparations for the Locarno Five-Power Conference. The British government has already notified the governments of France, Belgium, Italy, and Germany, which are parties to the Locarno Treaty, that the note proposes that the Five-Power Conference should first resolve various issues related to Western Europe, and then also address other issues in Europe. The initiation of the Five-Power Conference was due to Germany's re-militarization of the Rhineland area on March 7 of this year. Subsequently, France, Britain, and Belgium held a meeting in London and decided to convene a Five-Power Conference to seek a solution. Therefore, the resolution of the Western European issue should take precedence over other issues. (Havas Telegram, 18th)

Germany Plans to Establish Anti-Soviet Front with Japan; Ambassador to Japan Suddenly Scheduled to Return to His Post; Will Recognition of Manchukuo Be a Condition?

(Berlin) Diplomatic circles here are speculating on the possibility of Germany and Japan establishing an "anti-Bolshevik" front, as German Ambassador to Japan Dr. Dirksen is scheduled to depart for his post on October 13. It is now believed that Dirksen was originally supposed to be transferred to the post of Ambassador to the UK, but his work in Tokyo has been so outstanding that it is difficult to let him leave his original position for long. During his participation in the Nuremberg Nazi Party Congress, Dirksen met with the German Ambassadors to Russia, Schlenburg, the UK, Ribbentrop, and the Ambassadors to France and Italy. He personally listened to Führer Hitler's fierce criticism of Bolshevism. Based on the speculation of people here, Dirksen's decision to return to his original post in Tokyo was made after receiving instructions to increase the common interests of Japan and Germany on the Soviet issue. It is now believed that although there will be no formal alliance or military agreement between Germany and Japan, it is hoped that Germany and Japan can lead the world in establishing an entire anti-communist front, which would be supported by France, Britain, and Italy. If Japan sympathizes with Germany's views on the Soviet issue, then Germany may deem it appropriate to officially recognize "Manchukuo." German Anti-Soviet Movement Only Verbal; Aimed at Internal Consumption

(Berlin) During the Nazi Party's annual congress in Nuremberg a few days ago, Führer Hitler and key Nazi figures repeatedly delivered speeches attacking the Soviet Union, criticizing the Soviet system and the leaders of the Moscow government without reservation. However, to date, these anti-Soviet speeches have not been manifested in practical measures. On the recent "Army Day" in Germany, the Soviet military attaché to the German embassy, Orlov, was still invited by Minister of Defense General von Blomberg to participate in the review. Orlov was also invited to observe the German Army's autumn maneuvers scheduled for this Sunday. In addition, German industry continues to exchange German-made machinery for Russian raw materials, and German banks provide long-term loans to support the development of trade between Germany and Russia. The Soviet trade delegation in Germany continues to operate regularly in Germany, and German industrial organizations even have specialized departments to handle trade with Russia. It is also noteworthy that the German embassy in the UK has formally stated that Germany has no intention of attacking the Soviet Union, and when rumors circulated that the German ambassador to the Soviet Union, Schlenburg, was leaving his post and returning home, the German government immediately denied it. From this, it can be seen that the anti-Soviet speeches made at the Nuremberg Congress are mainly for internal consumption, not external. Moreover, since Bismarck, the tradition of German diplomacy has been to form an alliance with Russia. German diplomats, industrialists, and military personnel still adhere to this tradition, believing that a German-Russian alliance may still become a reality in the future. Furthermore, the German-Russian Friendship Treaty signed in Berlin on April 24, 1926, by the late German Foreign Minister Stresemann and representatives of the Soviet government, has been renewed every year since the Nazi Party came to power, without interruption to this day. This is also worth noting. (Havas Telegram, 18th)

The route within Yugoslavia that needs to connect with the Romanian railway has also been surveyed. Poland Recruits 100,000 Volunteers; Response to Germany's Extension of Military Service

Warsaw: The government announced the establishment of a voluntary work system at the beginning of this week. This measure is actually a response to Germany's extension of military service. Germany announced last month that it would increase the length of military service from one year to two years, thereby doubling the number of regular troops. However, the original length of military service in Poland was two years, so it was not convenient to increase it to three years. Therefore, the voluntary work system was created to make up for the deficiency. Most of those who participate in this voluntary work team will be the unemployed. It is expected that 100,000 voluntary work team members can be recruited soon. Therefore, from a social point of view, this move can reduce the number of unemployed, which is also of equal importance. Moreover, it is obvious that Poland took this step out of necessity for national defense after Germany increased its military strength. (Havas Telegram, 18th)

(Tokyo) The appeal of the so-called "Five Private Railway Incidents," involving former Railway Minister Heikichi Ogawa and eight others, which shook society to its core as the highest point of the five major Showa bribery cases, was reviewed by the Criminal Division Three of the Supreme Court, with Judge-President Komobuchi and Prosecutor Takeshi Matsu presiding. Hurricane Strikes US Atlantic Coast; Dozens Dead; New York Residents Stay Awake All Night to Prevent Disasters; Ships Along the Coast Struggle in the Waves

(New York) Skyscrapers throughout New York City were battered by a hurricane with winds of 60 miles per hour, and coastal areas were hit by huge waves. Residents throughout the city stayed up all night to prevent disasters from happening. At the moment, the entire Atlantic coast is under the assault of a violent hurricane, the intensity of which is unprecedented. Residents of many small islands are cut off from transportation to the city. As of now, there are 41 confirmed deaths, 67 missing, and many ships are reported missing or still struggling to stay afloat in the raging waves. Last night, a plane dropped flares from the air in an attempt to find a landing spot on Long Island, but it was unsuccessful. (Reuters Telegram, 18th)

(London) The port of Malaga, located 65 miles northeast of Gibraltar, which faced a serious situation yesterday due to infighting among government troops, is calm today. The new civil administrator and the army commander have arrived from Madrid to take up their posts. Two thousand government troops were dispatched in response to the appeal of the new civil administrator, Vargas, and are expected to arrive at the port today. (Reuters Telegram, 19th)

(New York) The coastal areas of North Carolina and Virginia are currently being hit by a hurricane from the Atlantic Ocean, causing significant loss of life and property. The situation is the worst it has been in many years. The wind speed in some areas has reached 100 miles per hour. Ocracoke Island, North Carolina, was hit by huge waves today, and the fate of the island's 400 residents is currently unknown. At the same time, hundreds of tourists at coastal resorts are fleeing inland in panic. Coastal patrol teams, naval vessels, and the Red Cross are on alert, preparing for the storm. Many ships at sea are being attacked by raging waves and are in a precarious situation. Coastal patrol teams have dispatched ships to provide assistance. Today, New York City is also experiencing a hurricane with winds of 100 miles per hour. Long Beach and New Jersey beaches, located a few miles from New York City, are being battered by huge waves. The scene is terrifying. To date, 41 people have died and 67 are missing along the eastern coast. Near the Delawar Bay near Ocracoke Island, North Carolina, a fishing boat was wrecked and sank, with 39 people missing. The safety of the island's 400 residents is a cause for concern, as they were unprepared for the arrival of the hurricane. (Reuters Telegram, 17th)

Cape May, New Jersey: A hurricane with a speed of 80 miles per hour struck the coast of New Jersey today. More than 40 people are missing, and six of them have been confirmed drowned. The whereabouts of the remaining 33 are still unknown. A fishing boat was rescued with five people, and several other ships are trapped between the coasts of Virginia and New Jersey. Two coast guard ships have now ventured into the sea to rescue them. Meteorologists announced this afternoon that the hurricane is now blowing northeast, and the North Atlantic coast may be spared. However, the danger has not yet passed for the coastal areas of Maryland, Delaware, and New Jersey. Among the coastal cities, Elizabeth suffered the most damage. Three major streets in the city are littered with rubble, and traffic has been completely cut off. However, there have been few deaths or injuries because warnings were issued in advance. Relief efforts are currently underway in the affected areas. The damage here is estimated to be over $250,000. (National Telegram, 18th)

(New York) Regarding the storm that struck the country's coast, the local weather station issued warnings several days ago. By last night, the Atlantic coast was swept by the storm. Newport, Virginia, experienced wind speeds of 160 kilometers per hour, resulting in 46 deaths and countless missing persons. In Norfolk, Virginia, the water depth on the streets reached one and a half meters. Houses along the coast were blown down, and crops were severely damaged. In this port, countless chimneys, storefront signs, and shutters were blown off by the wind, but there were no deaths or injuries. A fishing boat off Long Island capsized near Cape May, resulting in the drowning of 42 crew members. Only three people were rescued. (Havas Telegram, 18th)

Two Armies Continue Hand-to-Hand Combat in Ruined Spanish Fortress; Rebels Fight Like Trapped Beasts After Mine Explosion; Government Troops Follow Up with Rain of Artillery Fire

Toledo: Part of the Alcázar Fortress was destroyed by government troops with a land mine yesterday, but it has not yet been completely occupied by government troops because a second land mine has not yet exploded. After the first land mine exploded, the streets inside the fortress were covered in rubble, as if an earthquake had struck. Huge rocks were blasted into the air and then fell on the roofs, smashing them. A car used by the rebels as an obstacle was blown into two pieces, one of which flew 200 yards away into the fire station. Yesterday, the fighting in the ruined fortress continued until dark. The remaining rebels were still using machine guns in the ruins to resist, preventing government troops from occupying the fortress. The bravery of the rebels is truly astonishing. However, government troops have moved light artillery to the front line to prepare for a final bombardment. It is believed that 100 rebels died in the land mine explosion, while government troops suffered 6 deaths and 12 injuries. Government troops are currently preparing to continue the attack at dawn. After the land mine exploded, the surviving rebels launched a fierce counterattack with hand grenades and mortars. Government troops, waiting for the second land mine to explode, retreated from the ruins because the rebels were fighting fearlessly and rushing forward, and ordered the remaining buildings to be bombarded with artillery fire, raining down shells and taking advantage of the opportunity to build strong obstacles in order to launch a new offensive. (Reuters Telegram, 19th)

Second Landmine Explodes: Rebel Flesh and Blood Fly, Southern Capital's Key Point is Safe

Madrid – A landmine planted by government troops under the famous Moroccan-style Alcázar fortress in Toledo was detonated yesterday, completely destroying the fortress. Government troops were then able to occupy it. According to eyewitnesses, when the landmine exploded, huge rocks flew into the sky and then fell onto the roofs of buildings, destroying them. Several hundred rebels, including women and children, had taken refuge in the cellars, so they were not injured. The rebels, after sixty-one days of siege, were exhausted, getting only one meal a day, consisting of a small piece of horse meat and a little bread. The situation inside the fortress was terrible, with rotting corpses everywhere. However, the rebels remained defiant and continued to communicate with the outside world by radio. Among them were cadet officers and sons of nobles. A few days ago, they held a banquet to celebrate the victory of the rebel forces in Talavera and issued a "Siege War Bulletin" on a typewriter. When the entire Alcázar fortress was blown into the sky by the landmine, a column of rebels advanced at full speed, only fourteen miles from the fortress. To avoid the landmine, civilians throughout Toledo retreated to a mile and a half outside the city at night, sleeping in tents in the fierce wind. The besieged rebels bravely awaited death, sometimes breaking out to try to stop the landmine experts from completing their work. The fall of Alcázar allows government troops to control the road directly to Madrid and the railway line between Alicante and Valencia without a fight, so this battle is of great importance. (Reuters, 19th)

Toledo – Government forces detonated a landmine today to attack the rebels trapped in the Alcázar Palace. The battle was quite fierce. Our correspondent has recorded the details as follows: After the large landmine planted by the government forces exploded, the shock troops of the People's Militia under the General Confederation of Labor bravely charged into the rubble in front of the Alcázar Palace and raised the Republican flag. At that time, because one more landmine had not yet exploded, the shock troops stopped advancing. The rebels took the opportunity to bombard them with hand grenades and mortars, slightly injuring Colonel Barceló, the leader of the government forces. The shock troops were ordered to retreat and instead used cannons to bombard the rubble field, with shells raining down. At the same time, the rebels were setting up machine guns and cannons, planning to counterattack the government forces. Then the second landmine exploded, and for a moment, flesh and blood flew everywhere, a horrific sight. At noon, the fighting subsided slightly. At 5 p.m., the government forces launched another fierce attack. By nightfall, the government forces had made significant progress. Many rebels infiltrated into civilian houses next to the palace through underground passages, but they were all killed by the People's Militia with hand grenades. It is not expected that there will be any more fierce battles tonight. In total, the government forces have suffered six deaths and twelve injuries. The rebels have lost about a hundred people. (Havas, 18th)

Toledo – After the famous Alcázar fortress in Toledo was destroyed by the government forces with explosives, most of the 1,200 rebels, women, and children inside were killed. The two bombs, each weighing 300 pounds, not only destroyed the fortress but also collapsed many houses in the city. After the explosion, shock troops and security forces of the government forces charged into the smoke and ashes with rifles and hand grenades to engage in hand-to-hand combat with the rebels. Sixty rebels were killed, and forty government troops were also killed. According to an investigation by the Associated Press, the fuse for the explosives was 200 feet long. Before the explosion, sirens and loudspeakers warned the people to evacuate quickly and demanded that the rebels release the women, children, and elderly. The explosives were buried directly under the cellar, so it is logical to assume that the women and children were the first to be affected. After the explosion, the west wall of the city collapsed first. At that time, smoke and ashes covered the sky, like a volcanic eruption. The government forces then began an eighteen-hour bombardment. The rebels continued to resist stubbornly, refusing to retreat. Finally, the government forces suspended their artillery fire and concentrated their forces on a new position, preparing for a final blow. Soon after, they began a fierce bombardment again, hoping to defeat all the remaining rebels. The government forces declared that they would need to bomb once more to completely destroy the fortress and that this would be carried out within days. (National News Agency, 18th)

Spanish General Confederation of Labor Suggests: Organizing a National Defense Conference, Changing the Political System to a Federal System, Nationalizing Banks and Church Property

Madrid – The detailed plan of the National General Confederation of Labor to reform the entire political organization of Spain was revealed today. Its contents are as follows:

(1) Organize a National Defense Conference, composed of five members from the Socialist Workers' Union, five members from the Syndicalist Trade Union, and four members from the Republican Party, chaired by Prime Minister Caballero.

(2) Change the political system to a federal system, with a defense council established in each unit.

(3) Reorganize the various government departments.

(4) Unify the People's Security Forces to undertake police affairs and organize a compulsory army security force as the basic strength for establishing an army inspector-general.

(5) Establish a people's court system.

(6) Implement the socialization of banks, liquidate usury, and abolish national and local debts.

(7) Implement the socialization of church property and the property of those who support traitors.

(8) Implement an active peace plan.

(9) The Syndicalist and Socialist organizations form a national alliance to implement this plan.

This resolution plan has now been submitted to various groups that support the government and are requested to immediately endorse it. (National News Agency, 18th)

Nanyang Commercial Inspection Group Negotiates Import of National Products in the Dutch East Indies

News from Batavia: The Nanyang Commercial Inspection Group, sponsored by the China National Industries Foreign Trade Association, has made a very positive impression since arriving in Java. The overseas Chinese community has given them a warm welcome. Under the leadership of Chief Gao Shiheng, the entire inspection group is cooperating with the Consulate General, the Importers Association, and the Batavia Chamber of Commerce to carry out various diplomatic activities that have attracted much attention. Traditionally, Chinese people coming to Java faced extremely difficult entry procedures. Although this Nanyang Commercial Inspection Group was not dispatched by official circles, the Dutch East Indies government has paid great attention to it. The Dutch Governor-General has specifically instructed all departments to provide hospitality, and all entry procedures have been given special treatment, making entry and exit extremely convenient, which has brought many benefits to the overseas Chinese. However, since the arrival of the inspection group, despite making various efforts to import national products, they are restricted by the Dutch East Indies controlled trade, with various goods having specific limitations. In the Dutch East Indies import and export statistics, the relationship with China is very low. According to the percentage of imports from various countries to the Dutch East Indies in 1932, China only accounted for 1.6%. Ranked by country, it was twelfth. In the same year, the trade volume from the Dutch East Indies to China accounted for 2.64% of the total exports, ranking tenth. China has always been in a trade deficit because sugar and coal, among other things, are imported in large quantities from Java. As for the Dutch East Indies' implementation of restrictive policies, it has its own standpoint, which is not to be discussed for the moment. But in any case, China is in a disadvantageous position. The inspection group's sole task is to obtain import licenses in order to receive orders. The progress is described as follows:

Dutch East Indies Restriction Trade Measures

The Dutch East Indies government, in view of the unrestricted dumping of foreign goods, which completely undermined the commercial position of its mother country, despite various international negotiations that had not succeeded, suddenly promulgated various restrictions and permitted import regulations in June 1935. The method is based on the quantity of goods imported by each importer from 1929 to 1933-35 as the basis for the permitted import quantity. In other words, the government distributes and grants the permitted import quantity based on the importer's previously reported import volume over the five years. Unfortunately, overseas Chinese compatriots paid little attention to the import business before 1933, mostly purchasing from European merchants and reselling to the local population, thus losing the opportunity for Chinese merchants to import on their own, which has caused many difficulties in doing business. Moreover, the Dutch East Indies government has entered into agreements with countries such as Britain and Germany to exchange goods, meaning that Britain purchases a certain amount of goods from the Dutch East Indies, and the Dutch East Indies must purchase an equivalent amount of goods from Britain at the same time. Therefore, the restrictive conditions for each type of goods stipulate that a certain quantity must be purchased from a specific country, while others can be freely imported from any country. China and Japan are in the category of other countries. Although there are no treaties established between Japanese goods and the Dutch East Indies, their low prices are sought after by Chinese and European merchants. Because purchasing European goods not only yields no profit but also risks losses, while purchasing Japanese goods is profitable. Chinese goods are between European and Japanese goods, making competition difficult. However, some Chinese goods can compete with Japanese goods. When an importer's own permitted quantity is used up, they may apply to the government for a special license. Since China and the Dutch East Indies have not established a commercial treaty, the only way is to remedy this situation based on this method. After the inspection group arrived in Java, European commercial firms also expressed various good intentions. However, merchants are only interested in profit, seeking low prices and profits, and there are no national boundaries. Therefore, the only hope is that domestic manufacturers can reduce costs and strive for competition, so Java still has a good market, which overseas Chinese merchants are looking forward to. If national products are the same price as Japanese goods, then they will naturally purchase national products without a doubt. This depends on the efforts of domestic manufacturers.

Opinions of the Dutch East Indies Department of Economic Affairs

Gao Shiheng, the head of the inspection group, specially accompanied our country's Consul General Song to the Department of Economic Affairs on September 5 for an informal discussion. The attendees on the other side were Shi Ganmoer, Director of the Commercial Treaty Division, Pu Ke, Director of the Commercial Division, and the Chief Secretary. Chief Gao put forward various opinions, stating that there is indeed a possibility of promoting trade between China and the Dutch East Indies, and according to statistics, Dutch goods are exported to China every year, while Chinese goods, even before a commercial treaty is established between the two sides, have extreme reasons to ask the Dutch East Indies government to allow imports to seek a balance of trade between the two sides. Although this inspection group has received generous treatment from the Dutch East Indies government, they have not been able to accept orders due to restrictions, so they requested that special licenses be issued for certain types of goods. The Dutch side replied that they would certainly strive to achieve this within the scope of possibility, but there are some items that must be imported from the mother country, or the Dutch East Indies government has already established conditions with other countries, so there are some difficulties in reality. The Dutch East Indies government does not discriminate against any country and hopes that there will be opportunities to develop trade between China and the Dutch East Indies at any time.

Letter from Chief Gao to the Department of Economic Affairs

The following is a translation of the official letter from Gao Shiheng, head of the Nanyang Inspection Group, to the Acting Minister of Economic Affairs of the Dutch East Indies: Your Excellency Acting Minister of Economic Affairs, since our inspection group entered your territory, we have received generous hospitality and various conveniences from your government. On behalf of the inspection group, I would like to express my gratitude to Your Excellency Acting Minister. Our country and the Dutch East Indies have had a long history of trade, and the relations between the two countries have always been friendly. I firmly believe that there must be opportunities to promote trade between the two sides. Our inspection group has conducted a detailed survey of the agricultural products and industrial raw materials produced in your country, and as a result, we believe that they are very suitable for our country's use. We have brought samples back to China and will find ways to use them at any time. As for our country's imports to your country, according to the statistics of imports over the years, although textiles are the most common, in fact, the supply still falls short of demand. As our inspection group visited your area, we negotiated various transactions with Chinese and European importers, but unfortunately, we were unable to do so due to the restrictions of your government's licenses. In order to solve the aforementioned difficulties, I, on behalf of the China National Industries Foreign Trade Association of our country, apply to Your Excellency Acting Minister for special import licenses for the various Chinese goods listed. I further hope to establish a permanent cooperation between the two countries and promote trade. Before a commercial treaty is formally established between the two countries, a certain amount of Chinese goods can be imported into the Dutch East Indies each year so that Chinese goods have the opportunity to prepare for import. Also, regarding the import of Chinese goods into the Dutch East Indies, there should traditionally be a certificate issued by an official Chinese institution. The China National Industries Foreign Trade Association is organized by Chinese exporters. In order to facilitate export procedures for its members, the association can issue export certificates. We would be grateful if Your Excellency Acting Minister would recognize this. I earnestly hope that this letter will be presented to Your Excellency Minister, and that you will respond promptly, and that our country's Consul General Song will forward it. I deeply hope that our two countries will establish a good trade record based on the glorious history of the past. This is the sole aspiration of our inspection group, and we want to achieve the goal with the greatest effort. We also hope that Your Excellency Acting Minister will provide assistance so that it can be realized as soon as possible. I wish you good health.

Various Items with Restricted Imports

The so-called restricted imports do not mean that the items cannot be imported at all. It means that only a certain quantity of a certain item is allowed to be imported each year, and this certain quantity must be distributed among several countries. For example, some types of cotton cloth must be imported entirely from the Netherlands, and some percentage must be imported from the United Kingdom. Dull and high-grade rayon fabrics must be imported from the Netherlands and European countries, while shiny and low-grade products can be imported from other countries (i.e., Japan and China). Only 2,667,000 kilos of light bulbs are allowed to be imported each year, but it is stipulated that at least 1,466,800 kilos should be imported from the Netherlands. Large towels must be imported from Europe, while small towels can be imported from other countries. Cosmetics are not restricted, but only 850,000 kilos of soap are allowed to be imported each year. Underwear, beer, glassware, cement, kerosene lamps, cooking utensils, pottery, ironware, etc. are all restricted. Seasoning powder, electric fans, tiles, toys, steel essence enamel, etc. are not restricted. All kinds of regulations are detailed, and it is not easy to understand them unless you are personally there. The inspection group is currently busy collecting materials, running around during the day and working late into the night to cope with the environment, in order to achieve a certain position in national diplomacy. Fortunately, the Chinese Consulate General in Batavia has conducted research on various issues and has quite sufficient information. Consul General Song has also made special efforts for this inspection group and has provided much assistance.

The Group Departs for Singapore on the 12th

According to the results of the negotiations between the group and the Dutch East Indies government, the oral talks between the two sides were very satisfactory. The Department of Economic Affairs is preparing a written reply, and generally everything is no problem. It is hoped that after the Nanyang Commercial Inspection Group comes to the Dutch East Indies, trade relations between the two sides will gradually increase. In order to reciprocate the overseas Chinese, the group held a banquet at the Great East Restaurant on the evening of the 8th to thank the overseas Chinese from all walks of life. Consul General Song and more than 60 guests from all walks of life attended. During the banquet, Chief Gao Shiheng gave a speech, encouraging the overseas Chinese to support the central government and establish contacts with domestic industrial and commercial circles to jointly promote the sales of national products overseas. With the strength of 1.2 million overseas Chinese in the Dutch East Indies, they will surely achieve considerable success. Leaders from various business circles also gave replies. The group boarded a ship for Singapore on the 12th. More than 100 people, including the Director of the Department of Economic Affairs, Dutch East Indies government officials, our country's Consul General Song, the Chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, and overseas Chinese compatriots from all walks of life, went to the port to see them off and presented flower baskets. The situation was very enthusiastic.

Guangdong Native Cloth Merchants Appeal Against Overlapping Taxation Asking the Bureau of Consolidated Taxes to Refund the Original Consolidated Taxes in Order to Reduce Costs and Compete with Foreign Goods

Guangzhou Correspondence: The Guangdong Provincial Department of Finance has begun to abolish harsh and miscellaneous taxes. It has been found that the house rent in various counties, the ash rent surcharge in Taishan, the brick rent surcharge, the export cattle and pig donations in Yingde, Qiongya, and Huiyang, the theater surcharge in Foshan, and the fishing tax in various counties have all been abolished separately. However, the export tax on native cloth, the only industry in the province, has not been exempted. It has been found that the old-style native cloth in Guangdong Province, such as summer cloth, red cloth, and ramie cloth, is mostly produced in Xingning and Chao'an. Machine-woven native cloth is mostly exported from Guangzhou Henan and Foshan. The former is transported and sold to various provinces and cities in the country, while the latter is sold to Nanyang and other places. Because imported cloth is dumped, the sales of native cloth have stagnated. As a result, the number of unemployed male and female workers who live by weaving cloth is almost 70% or 80%. The Guangdong native cloth industry has become like a dying ember. General native cloth merchants believe that at this time of decline in the native cloth industry, the government should take measures to provide relief. However, the customs still levies export tax on native cloth, which is a major blow to the export of native cloth. Repeated requests for exemption have not been approved. The Guangzhou Native Cloth Industry Association recently stated that according to the Ministry of Finance's regulations, if native cloth is woven from raw materials that have already paid consolidated tax and is transported for export after paying export tax, the consolidated tax can be refunded. It presented a petition to the Guangdong, Guangxi, and Fujian Regional Bureau of Consolidated Taxes, requesting a tax refund. The original petition stated: "The petition is for already taxed and re-taxed, forming a double tax. We sincerely request that you grant a duty-free certificate and refund the consolidated tax to facilitate transportation and sales. We have secretly investigated that the cotton yarn used by pure weaving factories in Guangdong Province all comes from Shanghai. Only a small number of them are imported from overseas. When they are transported to Guangdong, they have already paid consolidated tax in Shanghai. The yarn from overseas also pays tax upon entry. Guangdong has no commercial yarn factories. Therefore, there is actually no cotton yarn in Guangdong Province that has not paid consolidated tax. All weaving factories under the association have little capital and buy cotton yarn in small quantities from yarn merchants, so it is impossible to obtain the original cotton yarn tax payment certificate. When the woven cloth is reported for export, because there is no original cotton yarn tax payment certificate, they must pay customs duties and cannot refund the original cotton yarn consolidated tax as usual, resulting in double taxation. In the past, your bureau considered the special circumstances of Guangdong Province and agreed to present a petition to the Customs Tax Division. Your bureau would stamp the export declaration form and release it duty-free. Your bureau issued the 39th order on March 24th of the 20th year to comply with this. It has been implemented for several years. Because the original consolidated tax cannot be refunded, there is a slight loss, but it is also convenient to be released duty-free. Since August 21st of this year, the Guangdong Customs suddenly charged 3 yuan and 90 cents per 100 kilograms of machine-woven native cloth reported for export. After repeated negotiations, they all said that they were handling it according to the tax administration's order and refused to make any concessions. We believe that all civilized countries in the world are doing their best to maintain foreign trade, reduce costs as much as possible, so as to compete with foreign goods and relieve unemployment among domestic people. Now, the cost of exporting native cloth from Guangdong to foreign countries is higher than that of selling it in the mainland. Is this the government's original intention to encourage exports and protect the industry? Moreover, the Guangdong weaving industry has been affected by the pressure of foreign goods dumping, the social depression, and the bankruptcy of rural areas in recent years. Its only chance of survival depends on the enthusiastic promotion of domestic products and the export of native cloth by overseas Chinese in Nanyang and other places, thus occupying a slight position. The association is planning to lead its members to work hard to improve exports and find ways to request the government to provide relief and allow the original cotton yarn consolidated tax to be refunded as usual to reduce costs so as to compete with foreign goods and live up to the enthusiasm of overseas Chinese in loving domestic goods. However, before the aforementioned goals have been achieved, the Guangdong Customs has added an export tax on native cloth, which increases costs under this double taxation. If no measures are taken to provide relief, the last chance of the Guangdong native cloth industry to export will be destroyed. For this reason, we earnestly request you to investigate and approve a flexible solution to the special circumstances of weaving factories in Guangdong Province, allow the export of native cloth to refund the original cotton yarn consolidated tax based on the weight of the tax payment certificate, or grant a special exemption from the export duty on native cloth as before, so as to avoid double taxation and save the Guangdong native cloth industry. Then hundreds of thousands of native cloth industrialists and merchants will be grateful." Respectfully presented to the Guangdong, Guangxi, and Fujian Regional Bureau of Consolidated Taxes.

Implementation of Drug Inspection and Compulsory Rehabilitation

In our county, the number of morphine addicts in the Eighth District exceeds 20,000. In order to completely eliminate drug addicts, the county government previously formulated implementation measures and submitted them to the provincial government for approval. Now, in accordance with the regulations, a drug rehabilitation center will be established in Datuan Town in the Eighth District, and a general team for reporting drug addicts will be organized at the same time. A deadline of three months is set, and the County Public Security Bureau is responsible for handling drug inspection matters. The bureau has organized seven companies and stationed them in Chenxiang, Datuan Town, Nicheng, Wanxiang, Bujia Shop, and Laogang. The bureau also stated that since all the drug inspectors in each team are male, there will be difficulties if they encounter women during inspections. Therefore, female drug inspectors will be set up in each team to specialize in searching and inspecting female drug addicts. Seven people have been recruited and assigned to each team. Today (18th), the drug rehabilitation center will open in Datuan. County Magistrate Zhang and Standing Committee Chen will personally preside over it. From the 19th, all drug inspection teams will start working. Anyone found to be a drug addict will be sent to the drug rehabilitation center for compulsory rehabilitation to break their addiction and will be exempted from punishment. If they commit the crime again, they will be severely punished according to law and will not be tolerated.

Teacher Electrocuted to Death

Xu Yucai, a teacher at Xiasha Elementary School in Taicang, recently purchased blood tonic because of his weakness. He planned to inject it himself. The afternoon before yesterday, Xu cut copper wire from a broken electric light wire in the school's spare room to use as a needle hole. Unexpectedly, the current in the wire was not cut off, and he was immediately electrocuted to death.

Suzhou

Holding an Air Defense Exhibition

The Wuxian Air Defense Branch is currently co-sponsored by six organizations, including the County Party Department, the County Government, the Public Security and Education Bureaus, the Security Brigade, and the Sixth Gendarmerie Regiment, to hold an air defense exhibition. In addition to various air defense books that have been made, they are also cooperating with the Youth Association to borrow various air defense models from the Shanghai Youth Association to be added to the exhibition in Suzhou. It is now scheduled to start at the Youth Association on the 26th of this month.

Water Police Team Encountered Bandits and Opened Fire

Zhou, the chief of the Second District of the Water Public Security Bureau of She Su, dispatched a team to join forces with the Water Public Security Bureau of the First District and the Zhejiang Water Police Team to suppress lake bandits. Zhou himself also led a guerrilla team to supervise the teams and search for bandits in Yangcheng and Dianshan Lakes. The day before yesterday evening, Chief Zhou patrolled from Dianshan Lake to Yangcheng Lake by steamboat and encountered three bandit boats. The bandits, seeing the steamboat in front of them, knew it was the police and turned around and fled. The police chased them to the Huayangpu area of Weiting. It was already dark. The bandits abandoned their boats and landed on the shore, hiding in the rice fields. When the police tracked them down, the bandits opened fire first, and the police also fired. During the exchange of fire, nearby villagers reported the alarm. Seeing the situation was not good, the bandits fled. The police searched for a long time but did not find them. They found an empty boat left by the bandits, with no one in it. They only found two earthen guns, one opium pipe, six flashlights, and some scattered items such as cigarettes in the boat. They took them all back to the district yesterday and continued to gather police teams from all over Dianshan Lake and set off again to search and suppress them.

Changshu

Eighth District Suffers from Rice Stem Borer Disaster Again

The area in the Eighth District of this county is mostly planted with late rice due to its low-lying terrain. After the area suffered from a rice stem borer disaster last year, the losses were heavy. Later, the province ordered the agricultural extension institute to be responsible for cleaning it up. At that time, due to the change of county magistrates, no one supervised it, and the borer removal work was not carried out as planned. Unexpectedly, when the rice was about to mature recently, it happened again this autumn because the borer eggs were not removed last year. The borer specializes in entering the rice stems, resulting in empty hearts that turn white and die. Now, countless numbers of Lizhi and Renyang towns in the area have suffered this damage. They have reported the disaster to the district office one after another. The district chief believes that the reports from each household are true and has telegraphed the county government on their behalf, requesting that personnel be sent to inspect the situation.

Wuxi

Completion of the Su-Xi Road Project

The Su-Xi Road project has now been completed. All compensation fees for graves and houses relocated along the route have been set by the Construction Department at five yuan per thatched house, two yuan per grave with an owner, and one yuan per grave without an owner. It is understood that a total of three thatched houses obstructing the road have been demolished and eighty-five coffins with owners have been relocated in Xin'an Township within the territory of Xixi, and a subsidy fee of one hundred and eighty-five yuan should be paid. It is approved to be drawn from the construction surplus funds. Yesterday, the Construction Bureau sent a letter to the Second District Office, requesting that personnel be sent to collect the funds and distribute them to each household.

Selling Counterfeit Drugs Being Investigated

The Xinsheng Pharmacy on Beimenwai Daqiao Street in this county is jointly owned by Wang Huaisheng and others. Its business has been good on weekdays, but it has been secretly selling counterfeit Sandelmidine tablets, which has been very profitable. The New China Foreign Firm, the general manager's office of the pills stationed in Shanghai, found out about this and sent a French employee, Pang Jiadun (transliteration), and a translator, Liu Xiqin, from Shanghai to Wuxi the day before yesterday to purchase a bottle of counterfeit Sandelmidine from the pharmacy. Pang and Liu, with conclusive evidence, immediately reported to the Public Security Bureau and requested that personnel be sent to search the pharmacy. Director Zhang, upon receiving the report, ordered Inspector Zhang Houyu to lead the police to inspect the pharmacy. They found a bottle of counterfeit medicine, a bottle of medicine pills without packaging paper, and a bottle of real medicine in the cabinet. They were all taken to the bureau for investigation.

Changzhou

Autumn Cocoon Trade Starts Collecting Cocoons

The Wuyi Sericulture Improvement Zone submitted a request to the Provincial Sericulture Improvement and Management Committee for approval of the number of cocoon baking stoves for the autumn cocoon trade. Soon, an instruction was received approving 768 stoves according to the sales of silkworm eggs and production. The Improvement Zone immediately announced that cocoon merchants should go to the zone to register by the 18th. There were still 36 stove quotas remaining. The Cocoon Industry Association originally scheduled to start weighing on September 23, but a few cocoon merchants started weighing on the 18th because the autumn cocoons had already entered the market. The price of cocoons was around 25 to 30 yuan per load. The goods have not yet peaked. In two or three days, all the cocoon merchants in the county will start weighing, and the cocoon market will improve.

Hangzhou

Major Fire at Wangjiangmen Last Night

Wu Yuanda Tea Shop at No. 42 Wangjiangmen Zhijie Street in Hangzhou City caught fire at 9:15 pm on the 18th due to careless tea baking, causing a sudden conflagration. The firefighters from the fire brigade rushed to put out the fire, and it took two hours to extinguish it. It is estimated that more than 20 stores and warehouses were destroyed, and a lot of tea was lost, amounting to 80,000 yuan. Yao Xingeng, the associate manager of the shop, has been summoned by the police station in charge, released on bail temporarily.

Collapsing Cart Driver Has Both Legs Crushed

Yu Jingfa, a cart driver at the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Zhakou Station, was working yesterday morning when he was hit and fell onto the tracks when the locomotive reversed and dropped the car head because he failed to avoid it in time. Both legs were crushed, and blood was flowing like a torrent. He immediately fainted and was carried to the railway hospital for treatment. His life is feared to be in danger.

Xiaoshan

Many Deaths from Drowning While Catching Tide Fish

Near Tiaoshuipu in Xiaosibu, Dongxiang, Xiaoshan, the tide has been very high recently, and there are many fresh fish that come with the tide. The sand people nearby who make a living by fishing in the tide, regardless of their age or gender, are fishing on the beach. Unexpectedly, the afternoon tide on the 17th was more than a zhang high. The general sand people who fish could not escape ashore in time, causing nine children surnamed Feng and Gao to be washed away by the tide. On the morning of the 18th, they were rescued along the river, and only four bodies of children surnamed Gao were found. The rest are still missing.

Correspondence

Letter from the Palace Museum

To Whom It May Concern: During the inventory of the Qianliang (money and grain) warehouse on the 14th of this month, the following items were found to be missing: item number 228, sub-number 2: 29 pieces of broken gemstones; item number 3: 30 pieces of broken gemstones; item number 5: one piece of purple garnet; item number 6: 16 pieces of turquoise; item number 9: one jade Ruyi scepter inlaid with three precious stones, with a box; item number 10: two coral branches, with a box; item number 12: one arched jade screen. After checking the handover records regarding the theft case involving Run Chang, the leader of the former Internal Affairs Department's resident guards at the museum, and the clerk Fang Jiqing, dating back to the 17th year [of the Republic], and after reviewing the lost item inventory of the Qianliang warehouse theft case, the missing items from sub-number 7 were all recorded. However, the list of missing items at that time was not limited to these. Further items will likely be discovered during subsequent inventories. It was found that in the old theft cases, some items were not re-examined at the time, resulting in the absence of a loss list for the stolen items in the records. Furthermore, due to the replacement of exhibits, loss of item tags, and relocation of items during the southward movement, after the change of museum directors in July of the 22nd year, a request was submitted to the Executive Yuan to dispatch personnel to oversee the inventory. This year, various organizations were also requested to send personnel to serve as temporary supervisors for the inventory to ensure impartiality. Once the entire inventory is completed, it will be carefully compared with the previous inventory reports and old records to obtain an accurate count of the items that are present or missing. Therefore, the inventory conducted in recent years, while representing the handover by the current director, also serves as a comprehensive investigation. As for the missing items from the Qianliang warehouse, silver warehouse, Cining Palace Garden, Imperial Workshop, Internal Affairs Department Hall, Jingqi Pavilion, Yongshou Palace, and other locations, they were all stolen in cases dating back to before the 17th year [of the Republic]. A thorough investigation should be completed soon. In order to prevent the outside world from mistakenly believing that theft is occurring at present, this detailed explanation is provided. It is hoped that it will be published in your newspaper to clarify the truth. Sincerely, National Beiping Palace Museum. September 15th, 25th year [of the Republic].

Bogomolov Hosts Banquet for Chiang Tingfu Last Night; China-Soviet Cultural Association Afternoon Tea Party Yesterday; Both Ambassadors Chiang and Bogomolov Deliver Speeches

Xin Sheng News Agency reports that the newly appointed Ambassador to the Soviet Union, Chiang Tingfu, has been busy with social engagements since arriving in Shanghai the day before yesterday. Yesterday, there were also the Saturday Club and banquets hosted by the China-Soviet Cultural Association and the Soviet Ambassador. Details are as follows:

Banquet from All Circles

Yesterday at noon, the "Saturday Club," an amateur organization of Mayor Wu and leaders from all walks of life, held a banquet at the International Hotel on Jing'an Temple Road to honor Chiang. Mayor Wu, Du Yuesheng, Wang Xiaolai, Yu Qiaqing, Qian Xinzhi, and fifty to sixty other people were in attendance. Chiang delivered a speech on the spot, and the gathering ended joyfully at around 2:00 PM.

Cultural Association Tea Party

The Shanghai branch of the China-Soviet Cultural Association and the Columbia University Alumni Association in the United States, represented by Jiaotong University President Li Zhaohuan, held a tea party at the New Asia Hotel on Tiantong Road from 4:00 PM to 6:00 PM yesterday afternoon to bid farewell to Chiang. Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Soviet Ambassador Bogomolov, First Secretary of the Soviet Embassy Saratov Chifu, Meramid, Chinese Secretary E Shan Yin, Military Attaché Lei Er, Commercial Representative En Qin, Deputy Consul in Shanghai Xie Manski, and representatives from the cultural and educational circles He Bingsong, Liu Zhan'en, Cao Liang, Wu Qingyou, Zhou Gucheng, Zhu Maocheng, Ou Yuanhuai, Wu Yun Chu, Zheng Shixu, Weng Zhilong, Yan Fuqing, Wang Yachen, Wei Ke, Jiao Jihua, Xiao Youmei, Wang Zhixin, and over seventy other people were present. Li delivered a speech first, reporting the significance of the reception and briefly describing the past work and future hopes of the China-Soviet Cultural Association.

Chiang and Bogomolov's Speeches

Then, Chiang stood up and delivered a speech, saying, "China and the Soviet Union are both vast countries with abundant resources and a long history and culture. Both countries are currently under construction and both advocate peace and do not wish to dominate others. Although the political and economic systems of the two countries are different, it must be understood that this is like people having different preferences, which does not prevent them from becoming good friends. The establishment of the China-Soviet Cultural Association can promote friendly relations between the two countries from a national standpoint, which is truly helpful to us." Soviet Ambassador Bogomolov then spoke, saying that the friendly relations between the two countries are based on mutual understanding, and the work of understanding is greatly related to culture. Therefore, I feel that the China-Soviet Cultural Association is extremely important. Mutual understanding between China and the Soviet Union will maintain world peace. This is not only a blessing for the two countries, but also a blessing for the world. I would like to take this opportunity to mention one thing: recently, German newspapers and news agencies have spread various rumors, such as the famine in Soviet Ukraine this year, conflicts between the army and the people, etc. I have already issued a statement to the Chinese press refuting these false statements. Previously, Chinese newspapers had published a statement by the Acting People's Commissar of Agriculture of Ukraine, Guguievsky, with statistics proving the falsity of the rumors. Finally, I must say that your country's former Ambassador to the Soviet Union, Dr. Yan (Huiqing), was stationed in the Soviet Union for three years and had a harmonious relationship with the officials and people of our country. He has laid a considerable foundation for Sino-Soviet relations. I believe that Ambassador Chiang will be able to promote and enhance it even more after taking office."

Li's Reply

Then, Shanghai University President Liu Zhan'en, representing the Columbia University Alumni Association in the United States, delivered a speech, saying that Ambassador Chiang had lofty ambitions during his study abroad years. Now that he has been appointed as ambassador to the Soviet Union, he has the opportunity to develop his abilities. We will certainly help him succeed with our spirit, etc. Finally, Li Zhaohuan replied, presenting three points, hoping that Ambassador Chiang will introduce more Soviet culture back to China in the future, and introduce Chinese culture to the Soviet Union. Some people from the China-Soviet Cultural Association plan to go to the Soviet Union for observation and speeches. He hopes that Ambassador Chiang will contact the Soviet government on his behalf after taking office.

Bogomolov's Hospitality

Soviet Ambassador to China Bogomolov hosted a banquet for Ambassador Chiang at 8:30 PM last night at his official residence inside the consulate on Huangpu Road, as the first official social event. Mayor Wu, Zhou Jue, Director of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Office in Shanghai, Yan Fuqing, Li Zhaohuan, leaders from all walks of life, and members of the Soviet embassy were also invited to attend. There was an exchange of views during the banquet, and the discussion was very pleasant. The gathering ended happily at around 9:00 PM. Chiang is scheduled to return to Nanjing on the 11:00 PM express train tonight to receive his credentials, await instructions from President Chiang, and then return to his ancestral home in Baoqing, Hunan. He will come to Shanghai at the end of next month and take a ship to Vladivostok to take office, accompanied by his wife and two sons.

Soviet Ambassador Hosts Banquet for Ambassador Chiang (International News Agency Photo)

Li Zhongchu Returns to Shanghai to Discuss Hunan Rice Transportation to Guangdong, 7 Million Dan Per Year

The rice market in this city is gradually becoming active as early and late rice harvests successively enter the market. The Hunan rice transportation to Guangdong issue, which has attracted national attention, has been completed. Li Zhongchu, manager of the Bank of Communications, returned to Shanghai yesterday morning. It is reported that 7 million dan can be sent to Guangdong each year. The details are recorded as follows:

Hunan Rice Transportation to Guangdong

According to investigations, Guangdong Province imports 10 million dan of foreign rice per year (each dan is 100 catties). Hunan Province has a surplus of 4 million to 5 million shi of rice in bumper years (each shi is 150 catties), equivalent to 6 million to 7 million dan of foreign rice. Guangdong Province originally declined Hunan rice because it did not suit the taste of the Guangdong people. However, through the advocacy and promotion of the heads of the construction departments of Hunan and Guangdong provinces, this difficulty has been completely eliminated.

Concrete Measures

The sales and transportation methods discussed by the two provinces were formulated by Yu Jichuan, head of the Hunan Construction Department, Liu Weichi, head of the Guangdong Construction Department, and Li Zhongchu, representative of the Bank of Communications. Li returned to Shanghai on a China Airlines plane yesterday to report the concrete plan this morning, with the aim of standardizing quality, reducing costs, facilitating transportation and sales, supplying in large quantities, and using financial, scientific, and political forces to promote it together. What has already been implemented is that Hunan rice is completely transported to Guangdong, exempting all miscellaneous taxes, reducing railway fees by half of the normal rate, and for ships (under the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company), Li has negotiated with the China Merchants Bureau for those entering Shantou. Guangdong and Shantou merchants have formed a transportation and sales company.

Improving Hunan Rice

For the improvement of Hunan rice quality, A. Production: (1) Organize cooperatives. Farmers initially form credit cooperatives. (2) Establish district and central agricultural warehouses. (3) Guide private boats to form private boat transportation cooperatives to undertake short-distance transportation between district and central agricultural warehouses. (4) Train rural workers. B. Transportation and sales: (1) Form a large-scale rice transportation company and establish Hunan rice transportation liaison offices in Changsha, Guangzhou, and Shantou, with three groups for agency affairs, introductions, mortgages, and settlements. (2) Establish new-style rice storage warehouses in Guangzhou and Shantou, with a standard storage capacity of 500,000 shi, and establish rice mills with a standard milling capacity of 10,000 shi per day, operating throughout the year. (3) Finance: Request banks to allocate low-interest loans at any time, the amount depending on the need (the previous proposal of a 6 million yuan allocation by the Bank of Communications in conjunction with the China Agricultural Credit Syndicate was only a proposal by Hunan Province). (4) Politics: Strict inspection. The Ministry of Industry should set up main agencies in Changsha, Hengyang, Zhuzhou, Lukou, and other places, and set up sub-offices or commissioners as appropriate to strictly prohibit adulteration and mixing, with quality grading attached. Currently, the most suitable rice for Guangdong sales is tentatively divided into four types: oil machine Special Grade, Tian Grade, Di Grade, and Ren Grade.

Local Rice Market

In the past, Hunan rice market prices were all based on Shanghai and Hankou markets. Now it has been decided to open an independent market price report in Guangdong Province every day. Rice merchants in this city and Hubei and Anhui provinces are worried that Hunan rice transportation to Guangdong will affect the markets in various places. The Huadong News Agency reporter investigated and found that there is no problem because Hubei and Anhui provinces also have the possibility of joint transportation. The local rice market is gradually becoming optimistic due to the successive entry of early and late rice into the market. The import of foreign rice has now disappeared.

Taxed Foreign Goods Distribution, Should Issue Resale License, Issued by Chamber of Commerce or Guild

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs instructed the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday, stating: "The case was received by the Municipal Government, and within the instructions of the Finance Ministry’s Customs Document No. 29654, stating the case was reported by the Fuzhou Customs Supervisor as saying, 'It has been requested in the letter of the Majiang District Chamber of Commerce that the style of import goods distribution license has already been given to us by your department, printed, and put into effect. However, this distribution license can only be used for transporting goods from Location A to Location B. After arrival, it must be handed over and canceled. If Location B wants to resell these goods to Location C, and then transport them from Location C to Location D, there is neither a customs transportation license nor a chamber of commerce distribution license. Military police along the way are bound to misunderstand. As such, there is no clear provision in the regulations for examination, so it is impossible to explain. Correspondingly, we hereby write, and would like to request a reply regarding how to handle these matters,' etc. After examination, the examination of what the Chamber of Commerce has requested to be interpreted is not clearly defined in the regulations. The matter concerns laws and regulations, so we dare not act on our own authority. What to do with the place that should be handled is hereby reported to the higher authorities for instructions," etc. The supplementary measures are now stipulated as follows: "For goods that have a distribution license, if they still need to be transported to other places for distribution after arriving at the designated destination, they should report the goods to the local trade association or chamber of commerce upon arrival, with the original distribution license, for verification and registration. When they are transported to other places for distribution, they should request the trade association or chamber of commerce to issue a distribution license according to Article 6 of the transportation and sales regulations for transportation. The same method applies to those who repeatedly transport to other places. (The style of this distribution license will be determined later.) In addition to the distribution, we hereby request that you check and forward it to the following for compliance,” etc. As such, besides distributing the order, we are sending out a copy of the license style for you to be notified and to inform the city’s Chamber of Commerce for their knowledge. This order," etc. Because of this, we are issuing the license style and ordering the Association to be aware of it, this order.

Large Number of Overseas Chinese in Russia Forced to Return Home

390 People Arrived in Shanghai the Day Before Yesterday. There have been several cases of Chinese laborers in Russia who have been forced to return home due to oppression. The Russian postal ship Northern, arrived in Shanghai from Vladivostok the day before yesterday, carrying 390 refugees, all from Shandong and Hebei provinces. In addition to the majority who are engaged in business in Russia and have a relatively affluent life, there are 68 who are laborers and are in a very miserable condition. They are temporarily residing in the Jiangxi Guild Hall, and the Shanghai Overseas Chinese Affairs Bureau and the Public Security Bureau have sent personnel to take care of them, conduct registration, and provide funds from the Overseas Chinese Affairs Bureau to send them back to their hometowns today. Personnel from the Public Security Bureau will also be sent to take care of them when they depart.

Qian Industry Held Managers Meeting Yesterday, Decided to Form Income Sharp Research Association, Elected Pei Yunqing and Other Nine People as Members, Compiled Opinions of Various Banks for Separate Research

The Shanghai Qian Industry Trade Association held an autumn managers meeting yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM at the association's location on Ningbo Road. The managers of various banks, Tong Yu Shaoyan Mountain, Yi Da Hu Chunxiang, Yuan Sheng Chen Qian Yuan Tang, Xin Fu Hu Hongsheng, Zhi Yu Liu Wuqiao, Yi Chang Xu Shouchang, Geng Yu Sheng Fanfu, Cheng Yu Wang Zhongchun, Jun Chang Zhou Chu Zhai, Hong Feng Zhu Shanbao, Heng Long Chen Yuqing, Wu Feng Zhang Mengzhou, Shen Yuan Lin Rongsheng, Zhi Xiang Jing Yongmei, Zi Feng Li Zhongxuan, Zheng Xiang Shen Dizhuang, Tong Run Pei Yunqing, Fu Yuan Xu Wenqing, Hong Xiang Jin Junyu, Heng Xun Xu Jingxiang, Shun Kang Lu Shuchen, Cun De Zhang Wenbo, He Feng Hua Jiguang, Yi Da Yan Dayou, Heng Tong Chen Hongqing, Hui Chang Hu Chuqing, Jiao Yu Zhao Songyuan, Zhen Tai Yao Chengchang, Qing Da Ye Xiuchun, Jun Tai Qian Yuansheng, Ding Kang Wu Zilin, Jia Yu Chuan Shenggui, Rui Chang Zheng Bosheng, Ren Chang Qi Ziquan, Da Lai Lou Huaizhen, Hui Feng Wang Yizhai, An Kang Ying Xinsen, An Yu Liu Zhaotang, Fu Kang Zhang Dafu, Hong Sheng Zheng Bingquan, etc., were present. Qin Xieqing, manager of the Qian Industry Reserve, was also present. Shao Yanshan chaired the meeting, and Ge Huaiqing recorded the minutes. First, the chairman reported that the securities deposit income tax will be levied on October 1. The association had resolved at the executive committee meeting to solicit opinions from each member bank on the income tax and limit them to sending their opinions to the association within one week for further processing. Now that the various banks have successively sent their opinions to the association, it was decided on the spot how to compile and study them and to form an "Income Tax Research Committee." The autumn managers meeting, executive committee meeting, and members' representative meeting each nominated three people as members. Pei Yunqing, Qian Yuansheng Wang Huailian, and three other people were immediately appointed as members. It was also decided that three more members would be nominated at the executive committee's regular meeting on September 25, and three more members would be nominated at the members' representative regular meeting on October 2. After the members are nominated, the committee will compile and study the opinions of the various banks in order to submit them to the competent state agency for explanation. The meeting adjourned at around 4:00 PM.
