Shen Bao Local Supplement Amateur Weekly

Life Guidance

How to Deal with "Chi Jiang Cha"?

— Xin Guifang

"Chi Jiang Cha" (吃講茶, literally "eat speaking tea") is a slang term, and by "slang," it's like the "old friends" of heroes in the old books, a popular term commonly used in the underworld. In Shanghai a few years ago, if you encountered a matter involving the "old friends" and had a small dispute that couldn't be resolved immediately, you would inevitably be taken to a place to "Chi Jiang Cha." This implied "speaking" to settle the matter, with "tea" serving as a gesture of respect to the guest. The original intention wasn't bad; it was actually an extremely peaceful means to turn big problems into small ones, and small problems into non-problems. At the appointed place (usually a tea house frequented by the "old friends," such as Yile Tian, Risheng Lou, Qinglian Ge in the city, or the "Sihai Shengping Tea House" commonly seen on North-South Shanghai Street), everyone would sit down, with covered teacups and teapots set out. After a brief greeting, they would drink tea and discuss the matter reasonably. However, times have changed. In the past, there was little shouting or cursing, and no one would jump around wildly. But recently, there has been a lack of restraint, and the so-called disputes often involve "chai shao" (拆梢, extorting) or "qiao zhu gang" (敲竹槓, blackmailing) – actions that make people feel sorry for the "old friends." As a result, both the municipal government and the special zone authorities have put up signs in tea houses "prohibiting Jiang Cha."

Currently, "Chi Jiang Cha" still happens frequently. However, some occur in hotels or restaurants; more modern ones even gather during tea dance time at small dance halls. Because they fear violating the law, they are very cautious. Even if outsiders walk by, they often can't tell that "Chi Jiang Cha" is taking place. They only see people whispering and discussing things privately.

As mentioned earlier, "Chi Jiang Cha" originally aimed to resolve disputes. Therefore, merely participating in "Chi Jiang Cha" isn't considered a serious matter, and it certainly shouldn't lead to a life-or-death struggle like enemies fighting. Thus, dealing with "Chi Jiang Cha" isn't difficult. Even if you are being "chai shao" (extorted), it's not a big deal. Sometimes, the "old friends" or loafers might misunderstand, or they might be "borrowing your reputation" by "kan xiang" (看相, sizing up) you, calling you a "yang pan" (洋盤, dupe), which in the underworld refers to someone not in the underworld, not "in the know," also called "kong zi" (空子, sucker), meaning they are not members of the Green or Red Gangs. But their established rules can restrain them and make them know when to stop (i.e., "shi xiang" 識相, knowing what's what). "Borrowing your reputation" simply means a free meal or drink, commonly called "la tai zi" (拉檯子, setting up the table), or "bang chen" (帮襯, helping out), which means asking for your assistance, asking you to spend some money, and everyone makes a friend. So, when they are about to invite you to "Chi Jiang Cha," they will definitely ask you first: "Do you have old friends?" If you can name a few old friends at this time (but you need to consider whether you have a real friendship with them; if you don't, you shouldn't randomly drag them in, otherwise, things will get worse), and the friendship is strong enough, then things will be easier to handle. Often, it can be resolved with a few words on the spot. Even if it's not resolved, when you arrive at the appointed "tea gathering" (tea houses where "old friends" often gather), if you bring the "old friends" you know along, one or two doesn't matter, everyone exchanges "qie kou" (切口, slang), and the matter can be resolved immediately. Otherwise, if your old friend gives an order (this requires someone with a little face), or sends two young guys to the scene, because the mediators have their own territories. If the friendship is strong enough, of course, they can go anywhere (the so-called "sihai" 四海, all over the world) friends who "dou de zhuan" (兜得轉, get around), from Longhua in the south to Wusong in the north, can visit each other anywhere). Otherwise, "guang gun bu dang cai lu" (光棍不擋財路, a bachelor doesn't block the path to wealth), and you need to clearly understand the principles. In addition, you should also use some indirect methods. Sometimes, two senior "old heads" with many followers might as well meet and explain the misunderstanding in person. This is "Chi Jiang Cha" between "old friends" themselves. The so-called "brothers argue within the walls" (兄弟閱於牆) often happens now, but it has very little to do with outsiders, so this article won't elaborate.

"A hero doesn't suffer immediate losses" (好漢不吃眼前虧) is something everyone can understand. The meaning of this article is to tell you: if you unfortunately encounter this sudden event, how should you deal with it? Earlier, I said that it's easier to resolve if you have old friends. But,

Page 22

what if you don't have old friends? The only way is to be adaptable. Because, if the loafers want to be very rude to you, they wouldn't bother inviting you to a tea gathering. The fact that they invited you to a tea gathering means they are still being polite. You might as well temporarily endure your grievances, show no emotion, or even be generous and amicable in dealing with them. You might as well indirectly lead them to reveal what they want from you. Because sometimes they care about face and won't mention money, eating, and drinking, but will talk about principles. This is their way of hinting that you should find a way to bring the discussion to the main topic, so you just bring it to the main topic. Of course, if you have old friends, that's another matter, because making friends always involves money, eating, and drinking. When you get to the main topic, you should make things clear in advance: you can talk about the bad economic situation, the lack of business, and although you appreciate the "old friends" looking up to you, your resources are limited. Of course, you don't dare to refuse the good intentions of the "old friends," and you hope they will forgive you, etc. On the other hand, you should observe the style of the people who came to "軋" (press, bother) you, such as their appearance, attire, and speech. Pay attention to who among them is the leader, or whether they always speak in unison. You should adapt to the situation and look for a way to step down easily. In short, never lose your temper; or stutter, unable to form complete sentences, revealing a completely weak demeanor. You must be soft but firm, firm but soft, carefully observe, and respond smoothly. If they clearly understand your financial situation, and see that you are not a country bumpkin, and that your words and actions are appropriate, they will also feel that making trouble unreasonably is not the way, and will gradually become frank with you. At the same time, admiring your fearless spirit, calmness in the face of adversity, courage, and intelligence will also stir up the chivalry and bloodiness of the heroes in the underworld, although sometimes money, eating, and drinking will cover up this chivalry and bloodiness. When you see this situation, that's when the opportunity comes. You must seize this point and state: "Everyone, 'a first meeting is like strangers, a second meeting is like old friends.' Although I haven't 'pressed' old friends in the past, I am willing to make friends with you all from this day on." I think this set of words, used to deal with the "old friends" for the so-called "yang pan" (dupe) or "kong zi" (sucker), is very suitable, beneficial and harmless. An ancient saying goes: "If you admit you are wrong first, people won't blame you; if you lie down on the ground first, who will hit you." To deal with "Chi Qing Cha" (eating invitation tea), you should remember this saying even more. If you want to fundamentally avoid these troubles, you can only restrain your own behavior in peacetime, so that people have no opportunity to take advantage of you!

Industry Practices

Silk Factory Foreman's Guide: Selecting and Boiling Cocoons

— Lizhen

As a silk factory foreman, one must understand general factory management methods, such as understanding the various personalities of workers, and methods of supervision and guidance. However, these are things that must be known to manage any factory, not just a silk factory. Secondly, one must know the general techniques of silk reeling, such as the temperature of the silk reeling soup, the volume of the silk reeling pot, the method of holding the cocoon, the method of reeling the silk, the method of increasing the amount of silk, and the method of increasing the efficiency of silk production. All these should be fully understood by the silk factory foreman. However, these have become specialized problems, and the content is very complicated, so it is not convenient to introduce them here. What I want to talk about now is a kind of work that the foreman must first know, and that is the selection and boiling of cocoons. As for the rest, you will gradually learn it after being a foreman for many years.

Before there were mechanized silk factories, we had already learned some primitive silk reeling methods in the countryside, such as boiling cocoons, baking cocoons, reeling silk, and adding silk. At that time, the methods were very old and simple, and not suitable for modern factories. Even the semi-mechanized handicraft factories and silk factories were generally simple and did not fully adopt scientific methods, so they did not require specialized knowledge and skills. But now it is different, and the selection and boiling of cocoons in silk reeling have become one of our specialized knowledge.

The fineness or carelessness of cocoon selection has a great impact on the silk yield project. Thin-skinned cocoons and cotton cocoons are related to the uniformity of the silk. Dead pupa cocoons and dirty cocoons (commonly known as blood cocoons) are related to the quality of raw silk. These are very important matters. However, the foreman should strictly warn: the general psychology of cocoon selectors is only that they think that the same cocoon, dirty cocoon, and dead pupa cocoon are related to the quality of silk reeling, and they select them out, but they do not pay much attention to cotton cocoons and thin-headed cocoons. If this is the case, no matter how complete the cocoon boiling method is, it is absolutely impossible to unravel them in the same way as good cocoons. As a result, the silk yield is reduced, there are more breaks, and the thickness is uneven. Those who have visited Japanese silk factories know that their cocoon varieties are better than ours, but cocoon selection is more meticulous than ours, which is worthy of our learning.

But what kind of cocoons should we select out? There are dead pupa cocoons, same power cocoons, irregular cocoons, cluster cocoons (the outside of the cocoon has firewood marks, or board shape, commonly known as firewood cocoon), dirty cocoons, maggot cocoons, cotton cocoons (this kind of cocoon, its silk layer structure is poor, easy to overheat when boiled, more tangled bubbles, the most bad), nutmeg-shaped cocoons, bald cocoons, thin-headed cocoons (this kind of cocoon is woven by the silkworm when it suffers from breathing in too much moisture or carbon in the air, opening a clear window at the top, becoming soup cocoons when reeling silk).

If you are reeling slightly coarser weave silk, you should pay more attention to thin-skinned cocoons, cotton cocoons, and small cocoons. On the contrary, if you are reeling slightly finer weave silk, it is easier to select large cocoons. The greatest impact on the color of silk is the silk and silk flakes reeled from dead pupa cocoons and dirty cocoons. The color of our country's silk is far inferior to that of Japan, and the value is also very different, which is caused by not paying attention to the stain on the silk.

The purpose of boiling cocoons is to make the silk soft and dissolve, so that it can be extracted in order, and on the other hand, it is good to make several strands of silk into a single strand, some are fourteen strands of silk and some are twenty-one strands of silk (that is, fourteen strands are combined into one strand, or twenty-one strands are combined into one strand), so the cocoons must be boiled with high-temperature soup. The outside of the silk strand has a kind of granular sericin, which is heated by hot soup, part of which dissolves in the hot soup, and part of which softens and expands, so that the glued silk strands are separated. Because the solvent of the soup medium is different, the solubility of sericin is also fast or slow.

When boiling cocoons, we should know the following: The first is the amount of cocoons boiled. If you focus on the quality of the silk, you can slightly reduce the amount. If you do not focus on the quality but focus on efficiency, you can slightly increase the amount. But an excellent cooker can boil slightly more cocoons, which is why he is more efficient. Cocoons that are easy to unravel (spring cocoons) can be slightly more, otherwise slightly less. Autumn cocoons with light cocoon weight and overly dry cocoons can be slightly less. In short, the amount of cocoons boiled is roughly one bucket of cocoons divided into ten or twelve times to boil.

The amount of water in the cocoon boiling machine is about five points up and down from the upper edge. The upper edge of the cocoon-containing crying should not be exposed to the air. Also, the water or soup in the cocoon boiling machine facing up should be supplied to eight points, and then steam is sent in. However, the capacity of the soup at this time expands due to the steam pressure, plus the distilled water that is cooled in cold water after the steam is added, and the water in the cocoon boiler is filled. The amount of soup, the shaking of the cocoon, the change of steam pressure, the turbidity of the soup, and the heat economy are all affected.

Also, pay attention to the concentration of the cocoon boiling soup. The ingredients contained in the cocoon boiling soup are the original ingredients in the water and the ingredients that are gradually leached out into the cocoon boiling soup as the number of cocoon boiling increases, such as sericin, protein and fat of the pupal exudates, and various inorganic components. The concentration of the cocoon boiling soup gradually increases, the concentration of water and electricity ions also gradually increases, and it becomes acidic. Therefore, the increase in the concentration in the soup, the less the dissolution of the sericin in the cocoon layer, the worse the unraveling of the cocoon, and the silk yield tends to gradually increase. The amount of the unraveling agent and the silk increasing agent added to the cocoon boiling soup and the silk reeling soup should also be changed according to the concentration of the boiling soup and the silk reeling soup. Therefore, the concentration of the cocoon boiling soup must be moderate. But this also depends on the quality of the cocoon.

The second is the temperature of boiling cocoons: the temperature of boiling cocoons varies depending on the time of boiling and the quality of the cocoons. Cocoon boiling is divided into three parts: pre-boiling, penetration, and post-boiling. The pre-boiling part (that is, the high temperature part) is inside and outside of Fahrenheit cold and heat, the penetration part (that is, the warm part) is inside and outside of one hundred and forty degrees, and the post-boiling part is inside and outside of one hundred and ninety degrees. The percentage of the time is 35% for the former and 65% for the latter.

As mentioned above, the cocoon boiling time has a high temperature time and a low temperature time, the former is short and the latter is long. If the cocoon quality is good, the sericin is easy to dissolve, the degree of dryness is high, and the cocoon boiling soup is light, the cocoon boiling time can be shortened. Conversely, it can also be extended. However, we should pay attention to the fact that the shorter the cocoon boiling time, the greater the danger. The same is true for being too long.

In addition, the protection of boiled cocoons, the treatment of boiled cocoons, and the steam pressure used for boiling cocoons must be paid attention to. Now we can put forward the general points that should be paid attention to when boiling cocoons. The steam pressure should not be increased or decreased suddenly. If it is morning or evening or during a rainstorm, you should be more careful. The interval between the cocoon container and the cocoon container should be 1 inch to 8 points. Before boiling cocoons, put three or four empty containers into the soup in succession, and then continuously put in containers containing cocoons to boil cocoons. Before boiling cocoons, carefully check whether there are any obstacles in the various parts of the machine. After boiling cocoons, be sure to sweep and clean. Pay attention to the degree of cookedness, and also maintain a certain degree of cooked cocoons to supply the reelers. In addition, the turbidity and amount of the soup temperature, the temperature of the barrel temperature, etc. should also be paid attention to.

Celebrity Interview

Du Chongyuan Talks About Prison Life

— Zhao Xu

I am very happy that I met Mr. Du Chongyuan unintentionally this time. Why do I say it was intentional? When the news of "Mr. Du's restoration of freedom" came out, I expected that the entire Shanghai press would inevitably go to interview him as usual; and Mr. Du would also refuse to see them as usual on the pretext of illness. Therefore, I intentionally did not join in the fun. In addition to making a phone call to ask Mr. Ding Huikang, the director of the Hongqiao Sanatorium, I sent a letter to the editor of this weekly magazine to ask about "how I could meet Mr. Du unexpectedly." He gave me a good idea. Sure enough, in less than five days, I met Mr. Du. It was during the luncheon when he was happily meeting with his friends.

Mr. Du is a man in his thirties, with a very burly figure, but a very amiable attitude, and a constant smile on his face. His accent is Liaoning with a bit of Beijing Mandarin, and his speech is loud and fluent. When one of his relatives introduced me to him, he seemed to limit the scope, saying: "I hope you don't describe this very ordinary experience of mine as a major event!"

I hurriedly said: "I just want to know about your life in prison."

Within this scope, our conversation continued.

"I heard that you were initially..." in the Caohejing Jiangsu Second Model Prison, and later applied for bail due to illness, and the Second Branch of the High Court designated you to be transferred to the Hongqiao Sanatorium for diagnosis. So, you were only in prison for a few months, and the rest of the time you were lying in the hospital, right?" I began to ask him.

"I was only in the Second Prison for four or five months, that's right!" Mr. Du said: "However, when I was in the hospital, there were also several sergeants and detectives guarding me."

At this time, one of Mr. Du's relatives told me again: "When he was detained in Caohejing, his wife, Ms. Hou Yuzhi, moved the... ancestral hall of the family (similar to...), so that she could send him food and miscellaneous items at any time. On the one hand, she ran around among friends to find ways to rescue him, and on the other hand, she filed an appeal with the Supreme Court. As a result of the appeal, the Supreme Court ruled that the appeal was allowed and the execution of the sentence was suspended. During the appeal period, he was still temporarily detained in the Second Prison. However, because he was 'awaiting investigation' and not a convicted criminal, the treatment was still good."

Mr. Du: "What was your life like in the Second Prison?"

"Besides eating and sleeping, I just read books." Mr. Du said: "However, before I went to prison, my life was too disorganized: I didn't eat at a fixed time every day; nor did I sleep at a fixed time. After entering prison, eating and sleeping had fixed times, so I felt I could take the opportunity to recuperate."

"What kind of books did you read?"

"I felt that in the past, although my blood, courage, and energy were not bad, I still lacked careful calculation. So in prison, I specialized in reading economics books."

"What else besides reading?"

"The time for free exercise was also set by myself and treated as a course."

"Then where was it held?"

"Originally, if..."

—When the authorities allowed Du to go to the Hongqiao Sanatorium for recuperation, Du (with ○) smiled cheerfully—

—Du was once imprisoned in a high-walled cell with a patio in the Caohejing Jiangsu Second Prison. Because the weather was hot, there was a reed awning over the patio—

Page 23

I was a criminal who had been convicted and interrogated with other criminals, then of course I would have to exercise with them at the time specified in the prison regulations. The place where I was detained was another separate cell, and there was a patio outside this room. That can really be considered a patio, because it was surrounded by high walls on all sides. I was active in that patio."

"Were you usually locked up in the cell?"

"No! Because I was an unconvicted prisoner at that time. Also, I am grateful to my relatives and friends: on the one hand, they asked the prison authorities to treat me differently; on the other hand, someone sent me a sleeping chair for sitting and lying down; and someone sent me a parrot in a cage. The parrot could call and speak, which could relieve my loneliness, and it was unusually tame. Sometimes you let it out of the cage, and it wouldn't escape."

At this time, one of his relatives said again: "At first, people sent him this 'caged bird,' and we were afraid that he would be more uncomfortable because he was emotionally affected by the scenery. Who knew that he loved this bird very much."

Mr. Du said with a smile: "This can be considered as sympathizing with each other!"

"I heard that the separate cell where Mr. Du lived was originally prepared for the famous international political prisoner 'Niu Lan' to live in. Later, he didn't come to live in it, so it was empty for some time."

"I haven't heard that said." Mr. Du's relative continued: "However, I once heard that a big foreigner lived there."

"Is the equipment there different from ordinary prisons?"

"There is nothing different!" Mr. Du's relative said again, "Only a canopy was built in the patio to protect against the scorching sun. Some of the furniture in the room was newly added, and he was allowed to bring more food, books, and small utensils, etc."

"Did people often visit Mr. Du in prison?"

"It was nothing more than his wife and her parents and the closest relatives, and they had to get special permission from the prison authorities. They also had to follow the regulations and could not leave or stay at will."

"Were they able to go to his cell?"

"After special permission, they could meet in the patio of his cell."

"What about the meals every day?"

"This was also specially prepared by... and sent to the prison after inspection, and then brought to the cell to eat."

"What time did Mr. Du go to sleep and what time did he get up every day?"

"There was a wake-up call every day in the prison. I got up when I heard the call, and I had to turn off the lights and go to sleep when the lights-out call was blown." Mr. Du replied.

"When did you get bail to the Hongqiao Sanatorium?"

"That was after the Supreme Court ruled that the appeal was allowed, and the weather was getting cold. I suffered from a severe cold and cough, so my family requested bail for medical treatment, and I went there after getting permission from the authorities."

"What was the living situation in the Hongqiao Sanatorium?"

"At first, it was diagnosis and treatment; later, I continued to recuperate. The rules of life were completely in accordance with the doctor's instructions. I didn't read books when I was diagnosed. I just took medicine, rested, slept peacefully, and ate some nourishing things every day. After I recovered a little, I started to read newspapers, take a walk, and meet with relatives and friends."

"Is it more free than in prison?"

"It's about the same. However, it is more convenient to eat and drink, and you can walk on the large terrace and lawn. Although a sergeant, Mr. Hou, is often with me, the environment is a beautiful suburban sanatorium, so naturally I feel much more comfortable."

"Can visitors move freely?"

"They can't. They must get permission from the sergeant and be with him to... talk."

"What did Mr. Du do in Jiujiang?"

"Is that a rumor in the newspaper?"

Mr. Du said: "Maybe because I used to run a porcelain business, so that's what they said? However, my body has not recovered yet, and I still want to recuperate for a while before I talk about it."

"Did Mr. Du's porcelain company develop well?"

"Before I went to prison, the one in the Northeast had closed down, and the one in Jiujiang is currently suspended. I am afraid that it will have to be greatly reorganized in the future."

"I heard that Mr. Du wants to travel to the interior, such as Hunan, Jiangxi, Guangdong, etc. Do you have this intention?"

"I heard that some of my relatives and friends want to invite me to Hangzhou... and said that if I want to go to Jiujiang, it would be better to travel from Zhejiang and Jiangxi... and then... that's how the speculation arose, right? I really haven't made up my mind myself."

Afterwards, I heard Mr. Du's relative say that his brother-in-law, Mr. Hou, who rushed to Shanghai because Mr. Du was imprisoned, has transferred to a middle school in Shanghai; Mr. Du's residence in... has not been unsubscribed. His wife, Ms. Hou, has also suffered from illness due to hard work and overwork. Her illness has now healed, but her body is still very weak, so she probably won't travel far for the time being, right?

I talked to Mr. Du that day and then left because of something, but unfortunately I didn't get to see him and his relatives and friends having a good time together, but the impression he gave me was deep enough.

World News

Wild Rabbits as a Pest

— Yun

On Australian pastures there is a small shrub whose leaves are the main food for sheep during dry periods. But at the same time these leaves are also a great food for wild rabbits, and without it, countless wild rabbits would not be able to survive during the drought. In this way, wild rabbits have become the most harmful thing in this area. The Scientific and Industrial Research Assessment Council of the area has concentrated its efforts to invent some of the most effective methods to eliminate wild rabbits, but the results still cannot eliminate them. According to the survey, this area spends millions of pounds every year to drive away wild rabbits; due to the abandonment of pastures by wild rabbits, the harvest of wool and mutton is reduced by 100 million pounds. At the same time, the skin and meat of the captured wild rabbits are only worth millions of pounds when exported abroad every year. Comparing the two, the damage is really great, so the people of the area feel deeply pained by the wild rabbits. According to their estimates, if the wild rabbits could be removed, the area's sheep production would increase by 25 percent compared to normal!

Common Sense

Delicacies and Health

— Ke

The wealthy in the city often eat delicacies and drink blood-tonifying wine, but they are either bloated or pale and rarely healthy. The farmers in the countryside often eat corn and vegetables, but they are mostly strong and healthy and free of disease. Furthermore, city dwellers have an endless supply of delicacies from land and sea, but unfortunately, they often suffer from stomach ailments. Many country and city folk also suffer from stomach ailments, but their stomach ailments are not due to indigestion but rather a deficiency of the stomach, lacking anything to digest. Based on these facts, we can draw two conclusions: first, eating good food does not necessarily make one healthy; and second, overeating and undereating both lead to illness, a characteristic of the current age.

According to a report by a certain famous American medical doctor, a businessman recently suffered from a strange disease. The symptom was that every day at 11 a.m. he would fall into a state of extreme sleep. No matter how much noise was made during his sleep, he would not wake up. Several times he had driven his car through crowded areas and encountered danger because the disease would suddenly strike, causing him to fall asleep. Many famous doctors investigated this strange disease but could not determine its cause. Later, they specially investigated his diet and discovered that he ate cream and coffee every morning. So, the doctor ordered him to stop eating cream, and the strange disease gradually disappeared. There was also a university student who developed a disease that caused pain all over his body, preventing him from doing anything. At first, it was thought to be a mental illness, but it was later determined that it was also caused by eating too much good food. Because he ate two to four eggs every day, he could not digest them, resulting in his serious illness.

Economic News

Germany's Oil Problem

— Chong

In its wartime economic development, the most important problem for the "Third Reich," which is diligently preparing for war, is the problem of fuel, the problem of oil.

Although Germany is a powerful heavy industry country, it does not have a good oil base. Recently, Berlin published a document pointing out that when the First World War broke out in 1914, the oil problem was not given special attention, so this problem caused the German authorities great pain at the end of the war. However, at that time, by strengthening the production of petroleum and coal liquefaction products, and by purchasing oil produced in Romania during the war, the problem was considerably alleviated. But now? The actual situation is fundamentally different. According to calculations by Berlin experts, the wartime organization of the German army has 300 divisions, including 30 divisions with 10,400 tanks and transport vehicles, 9,000 aircraft, and mechanized divisions equipped with airfields and air defense equipment. The displacement of naval warships and seaplanes is 500,000 to 600,000 tons. Thus, Germany's wartime fuel needs are estimated to be more than 12 million tons per year. However, Germany's domestic fuel production in 1934 was only 850,000 tons, and last year it only increased to 1.1 million to 1.15 million tons. This large gap between needs and production fully demonstrates that Germany's current oil problem is much more serious than during the last war.

Currently, Germany is in the development phase of war preparations, and the production of automobiles and transport vehicles is increasing daily. According to statistics, automobile production in 1932 was 43,400 vehicles, which increased to 201,400 vehicles last year. The production of transport vehicles in 1932 was 8,000 vehicles, which increased to 38,800 vehicles last year. In addition, the production of aircraft and tanks has also greatly increased. In this way, Germany's fuel needs are naturally increasing.

Once a war breaks out, commercial relations between the belligerents will be completely severed, and oil, as an important military material, will naturally be embargoed. Germany's domestic oil production is so weak, and its needs are so great. If a war breaks out and there are problems with the import of foreign oil, then the "Second Reich's" cars and tanks will not be able to move, aircraft will not be able to fly high, and full mobilization of warships will be difficult. What a terrible danger! Therefore, in recent years, the National Socialist government has been doing everything possible to increase oil production in order to achieve German oil self-sufficiency. We can specifically discuss a few points:

First, the extraction of crude oil. Since 1934, the German government has been working to expand oil producing areas. In that year, the government spent huge amounts of subsidies, adding 54 new oil wells, covering an area of 53 kilometers. Later, it increased to 85 wells, expanding the area to 99 kilometers. Last October, many new oil producing areas were discovered, which of course further expanded the area of oil producing areas. As a result, Germany's crude oil production last year almost doubled compared to 1933 (Editor's note: Production in 1933 was 219,000 tons, and in 1935 it was 430,000 tons).

However, this increase in crude oil production came at a great cost. Moreover, the quality of these crude oils is only suitable for refining lubricating oil and is not very suitable for fuel. So, although the quantity has increased, it is of little benefit to Germany, which is preparing for war.

Second, the production of petroleum and other coal carbonization products. Currently, Germany has 40 million tons of lignite production, all of which is used for this purpose. According to Dr. Hurotai's calculations, in theory, 1.6 million tons of black mineral oil can be extracted from it, and 960,000 tons of petroleum, 200,000 tons of fuel black mineral oil, and 50,000 tons of lubricating oil can be extracted from it. However, when theoretical calculations are moved to practical implementation, many difficulties arise. The result is only a small increase in fuel production, and the problem is not solved at all. At the same time, the forced implementation of this artificial method consumes too much, which further increases the wartime budget and creates more problems for the national finances.

Third, efforts to liquefy coal. This method has gone through many difficulties, and only now has it achieved some results. Therefore, the German military has great hope for the production of coal-liquefied oil, fantasizing that it can solve Germany's fuel problem. However, judging from the recent situation, that fantasy will probably forever remain a fantasy. For example, the various chemicals and raw materials required in coal liquefaction cannot be smoothly resolved first.

In short, under the current circumstances, the German government will try every means that can be used to extract oil and produce fuel. For example, efforts to produce alcohol and gas are aimed at increasing the supply of fuel. However, every artificial fuel manufacturing method has the problem of excessively high production costs. Products with such high production costs naturally cannot compete with foreign goods in the German market. Therefore, the German government specially uses tariffs to protect domestic oil. However, in this way, the "Third Reich's" tariff revenue has suffered a great loss. At the same time, because Germany needs a large amount of oil, even if its domestic oil production increases annually, and even if it uses tariffs to protect domestic oil, a large amount of oil is still imported into Germany in recent years. According to statistics, Germany's fuel imports in 1933 were 2.65 million tons, and by last year, they had increased to 3.77 million tons. This year's statistics are certainly more than this. Judging from this simple statistic alone, we can also know the seriousness of Germany's current oil problem.

In order to increase the production of oil fuel, in addition to the above-mentioned artificial methods of manufacturing oil and fuel, the German government previously combined the ten major lignite companies with 250 million marks to strive to produce petroleum. Recently, it was decided to invest huge amounts of funds in 1936 and 1937. According to their estimates, under many favorable conditions, Germany can produce 1 million tons of synthetic petroleum in 1937. However, this is still a very small number compared to the amount of fuel Germany needs in wartime as described above. This situation clearly tells us that Germany's efforts to achieve oil self-sufficiency have been declared a failure.

Due to war preparations, due to the lack of oil, and due to the failure of efforts to achieve oil self-sufficiency, Germany has to pay more attention to choosing allies in future wars. In this selection, it is necessary to find a country with abundant oil production, which has led to the emergence of pro-British and pro-American factions in the German military. At the same time, Romania, in the Little Entente, also has abundant oil production, and therefore the country has also been quite attentive to Hitler. Recently, the reorganization of the Romanian cabinet has shown a pro-German tendency. It is argued that this is the effect of the National Socialist Party. If so, it further demonstrates that Germany's oil problem is not only a major domestic problem, but also has a deep relationship with Germany's diplomacy and, therefore, with international political economy.

Natural Science Lecture

Revision of the Law of Universal Gravitation

— Enlightenment

In the physics textbooks currently used in schools, the basic principles of mechanics are still based on Newton's three laws of motion, and Newton's "Law of Universal Gravitation" is still being reviewed in the same old way, with no new elements added. Except for some common sense of new mechanical principles that have been heard or introduced in some specialized natural science magazines, the lecture halls of the science department of the university still use the original Western version of the 19th century for lectures, which cannot but be regretted by our academic and educational circles!

Before talking about the revision of Newton's law of universal gravitation, we might as well describe the general idea of universal gravitation.

One day, when Newton was playing in the park, he happened to see an apple falling to the ground from a tree, and thus he realized the earth's attraction, thinking that the fall of the apple was due to the attraction of the earth's center. Extending this further, he also thought that the rotation of the earth and other planets around the sun without separation was also due to the sun's attraction of the earth and other planets. Similarly, the moon's orbit around the earth, the orbits of other satellites around other planets, and the attachment of various objects on the earth to the earth are all due to this reason. Therefore, the theory of universal gravitation was derived, and its law is as follows:

In the universe, relative objects attract each other, regardless of their distance. The magnitude of the force is directly proportional to the product of the masses of the objects and inversely proportional to the square of their distance.

The product of the mass of the earth is greater than the product of the masses of various objects on the earth's surface, and the distance is the closest. Therefore, the apple must fall on the earth's surface, and not on the moon's surface, nor on the surface of the sun or its planets. The moon must depend on the earth, and the earth and other planets must orbit the sun. According to universal gravitation, plus the attraction and repulsion of the mutual attraction and repulsion forces, it can also be proven. Newton's law of universal gravitation is roughly as described above. This is the mechanical principle that has been regarded as the benchmark by the mechanics community for a hundred years.

But all academics are advancing, and they are constantly evolving, and the law of universal gravitation is no exception.

Before talking about the revision of the law of universal gravitation, we might as well first describe the situation of the new mechanics produced from the old mechanics. The foundation of the old mechanics is Newton's law of motion. This law requires assuming an absolutely stationary reference body in the universe as the coordinate for measuring the moving body. But now we know that this hypothesis is unreasonable, because the "ether" that he used as the absolutely stationary reference body has long been proven unnecessary and mysterious in modern physics. There is absolutely no non-object and non-moving thing in space. Furthermore, the old mechanics believed that length, time, and mass are constant and invariable. But now it has long been proven that these three change during the movement process and are relatively defined. The old mechanics' concept of force assumes an absolutely stationary reference body. An object with acceleration relative to the reference body is subject to force. Now that there is no need to assume this absolutely stationary reference body, natural phenomena must be examined with the observer as the standard, so the concept of mechanics must be revised from the beginning.

For example, passengers on an airplane seem to feel their weight decreasing when they start to descend. If the plane descends at "gravitational acceleration," the passenger will feel as if he has completely lost his weight. If you look at it from a standard body outside the plane, then the passenger is moving at "gravitational speed," and at the same time, it can be said that he is subject to the action of gravity. However, if the passenger takes himself as the standard and does not look outside, then he does not even know his own movement, and his own weight - that is, the gravity exerted on himself
